For classes that are either not found or are not supposed to\n * be loaded in isolation, this plugin classloader delegates their loading to its parent. This makes\n * this classloader a child-first classloader.\n * <p>\n * This class is thread-safe and parallel capable.\n */\npublic class PluginClassLoader extends URLClassLoader {\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(PluginClassLoader.class);\n    private final URL pluginLocation;\n\n    static {\n        ClassLoader.registerAsParallelCapable();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Constructor that accepts a specific classloader as parent.\n     *\n     * @param pluginLocation the top-level location of the plugin to be loaded in isolation by this\n     * classloader.\n     * @param urls the list of urls from which to load classes and resources for this plugin.\n     * @param parent the parent classloader to be used for delegation for classes that were\n     * not found or should not be loaded in isolation by this classloader.\n     */\n    public PluginClassLoader(URL pluginLocation, URL[] urls, ClassLoader parent) {\n        super(urls, parent);\n Objects.requireNonNull(name);\n\n        URL url = findResource(name);\n        if (url == null) {\n            url = super.getResource(name);\n        }\n        return url;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Enumeration<URL> getResources(String name) throws IOException {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(name);\n        List<URL> resources = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (Enumeration<URL> foundLocally = findResources(name); foundLocally.hasMoreElements();) {\n            URL url = foundLocally.nextElement();\n            if (url != null)\n                resources.add(url);\n        }\n        // Explicitly call the parent implementation instead of super to avoid double-listing the local resources\n        for (Enumeration<URL> foundByParent = getParent().getResources(name); foundByParent.hasMoreElements();) {\n            URL url = foundByParent.nextElement();\n            if (url != null)\n                resources.add(url);\n        }\n        return Collections.enumeration(resources);\n    }\n\n    // This method needs to be thread-safe because it is supposed to be called by multiple\n    // Connect tasks. While findClass is thread-safe, defineClass called within loadClass of the\n    // base method is not. More on multithreaded classloaders in:\n    // https://docs.oracle.com/javase/7/docs/technotes/guides/lang/cl-mt.html\n    @Override\n    protected Class<?> loadClass(String name, boolean resolve) throws ClassNotFoundException {\n        synchronized (getClassLoadingLock(name)) {\n            Class<?> klass = findLoadedClass(name);\n            if (klass == null) {\n                try {\n                    if (PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation(name)) {\n                        klass = findClass(name);\n                    }\n                } catch (ClassNotFoundException e) {\n                    // Not found in loader's path. Search in parents.\n                    log.trace(\"Class '{}' not found. Delegating to parent\", name);\n                }\n            }\n            if (klass == null) {\n                klass = super.loadClass(name, false);\n            }\n            if (resolve) {\n                resolveClass(klass);\n            }\n            return klass;\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":135,"startLine":1,"totalLines":135}}}

dependency injection mechanism through interface-based plugin architecture and classloader isolation. The system is centered in the `org.apache.kafka.connect.runtime.isolation` package.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Loading Infrastructure\\n\\nThe **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java) is a custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading isolation. It extends URLClassLoader and uses the loadClass() method with synchronized locking to ensure thread-safe class loading while isolating plugin classes from the main application.\\n\\nThe **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java) manages the hierarchy of plugin classloaders. It maintains a ConcurrentMap of plugin descriptors and delegates class loading to appropriate PluginClassLoader instances, using the PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation() method to determine which classes should be loaded in isolation.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe **PluginScanner** abstract class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java) provides the foundation for plugin discovery through the discoverPlugins() method, which scans PluginSource instances and returns a PluginScanResult.\\n\\nTwo concrete implementations provide different discovery strategies:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java) - Uses the ClassGraph library to perform reflective scanning of all classes in plugin jars, discovering classes that implement plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate).\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java) - Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins based on META-INF/services manifest files, which is the modern, performant approach for plugin discovery.\\n\\nBoth scanners validate that discovered classes are concrete, public, have public no-args constructors, and are subclasses of the supported plugin types.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Dependency Injection\\n\\nThe dependency injection system relies on the **Configurable** mixin interface (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java), which defines a single configure(Map<String, ?> configs) method. This interface is implemented by:\\n\\n1. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java) - Extends Configurable for header conversion, implementing fromConnectHeader() and toConnectHeader() methods.\\n\\n2. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java) - Extends Configurable for message transformations, implementing the apply() method for record transformation.\\n\\n3. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java) - Extends Configurable for conditional record matching, implementing the test() method.\\n\\nThe **Converter** interface (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java) has its own configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey) method signature for key/value distinction.\\n\\nThe **Connector** abstract base class (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java) receives configuration through its start(Map<String, String> props) method. Task implementations similarly receive configuration through their start() methods.\\n\\n## Plugin Management\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) orchestrates the entire plugin loading system. Its initLoaders() method coordinates plugin discovery using either ReflectionScanner or ServiceLoaderScanner based on the PluginDiscoveryMode, then installs discovered plugins into the DelegatingClassLoader.\\n\\nThe **PluginDesc** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java) stores metadata about each discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type (from the PluginType enum), and classloader.\\n\\nThe **PluginScanResult** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java) aggregates discovered plugins by type: SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, and ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.\\n\\n## Isolation Mechanism\\n\\nThe **PluginUtils** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) contains the shouldLoadInIsolation() method which determines which classes should be loaded through isolated plugin classloaders. This uses inclusion/exclusion patterns to identify plugin classes while excluding standard Java and Kafka classes.\\n\\nThe **LoaderSwap** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) manages thread context classloader swaps during plugin instantiation to ensure plugins are initialized with the correct classloader context.\\n\\nThis architecture achieves complete plugin isolation while enabling dependency injection through interface implementation and configuration callbacks, allowing plugins to be discovered dynamically and configured at runtime without requiring modifications to the core Kafka Connect system.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1835,"cache_read_input_tokens":57662,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1835},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3924602d-6d1d-451e-84e5-df77165299cd","uuid":"7f464d44-43c3-4546-b06c-fbc27ffaab4b"}

\"clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java\", \"symbol\": \"configure\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Apache Kafka's plugin/extension loading system implements a sophisticated Java dependency injection mechanism through interface-based plugin architecture and classloader isolation. The system is centered in the `org.apache.kafka.connect.runtime.isolation` package.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Loading Infrastructure\\n\\nThe **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java) is a custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading isolation. It extends URLClassLoader and uses the loadClass() method with synchronized locking to ensure thread-safe class loading while isolating plugin classes from the main application.\\n\\nThe **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java) manages the hierarchy of plugin classloaders. It maintains a ConcurrentMap of plugin descriptors and delegates class loading to appropriate PluginClassLoader instances, using the PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation() method to determine which classes should be loaded in isolation.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe **PluginScanner** abstract class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java) provides the foundation for plugin discovery through the discoverPlugins() method, which scans PluginSource instances and returns a PluginScanResult.\\n\\nTwo concrete implementations provide different discovery strategies:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java) - Uses the ClassGraph library to perform reflective scanning of all classes in plugin jars, discovering classes that implement plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate).\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java) - Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins based on META-INF/services manifest files, which is the modern, performant approach for plugin discovery.\\n\\nBoth scanners validate that discovered classes are concrete, public, have public no-args constructors, and are subclasses of the supported plugin types.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Dependency Injection\\n\\nThe dependency injection system relies on the **Configurable** mixin interface (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java), which defines a single configure(Map<String, ?> configs) method. This interface is implemented by:\\n\\n1. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java) - Extends Configurable for header conversion, implementing fromConnectHeader() and toConnectHeader() methods.\\n\\n2. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java) - Extends Configurable for message transformations, implementing the apply() method for record transformation.\\n\\n3. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java) - Extends Configurable for conditional record matching, implementing the test() method.\\n\\nThe **Converter** interface (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java) has its own configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey) method signature for key/value distinction.\\n\\nThe **Connector** abstract base class (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java) receives configuration through its start(Map<String, String> props) method. Task implementations similarly receive configuration through their start() methods.\\n\\n## Plugin Management\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) orchestrates the entire plugin loading system. Its initLoaders() method coordinates plugin discovery using either ReflectionScanner or ServiceLoaderScanner based on the PluginDiscoveryMode, then installs discovered plugins into the DelegatingClassLoader.\\n\\nThe **PluginDesc** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java) stores metadata about each discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type (from the PluginType enum), and classloader.\\n\\nThe **PluginScanResult** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java) aggregates discovered plugins by type: SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, and ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.\\n\\n## Isolation Mechanism\\n\\nThe **PluginUtils** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) contains the shouldLoadInIsolation() method which determines which classes should be loaded through isolated plugin classloaders. This uses inclusion/exclusion patterns to identify plugin classes while excluding standard Java and Kafka classes.\\n\\nThe **LoaderSwap** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) manages thread context classloader swaps during plugin instantiation to ensure plugins are initialized with the correct classloader context.\\n\\nThis architecture achieves complete plugin isolation while enabling dependency injection through interface implementation and configuration callbacks, allowing plugins to be discovered dynamically and configured at runtime without requiring modifications to the core Kafka Connect system.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
